116void toolbox::blockstructured::tests::IandRVolumetricTest::
117 testSecondOrderInterpolation() {
118
119 constexpr int NumberOfUnknowns = 1;
120 constexpr int sourceHaloSize = 3;
121 constexpr int destinationHaloSize = 1;
122
123 for (int destinationPatchSize = 2; destinationPatchSize < 5;
124 destinationPatchSize++) {
125 for (int sourcePatchSize = 2; sourcePatchSize < destinationPatchSize;
126 sourcePatchSize++) {
127
128#if Dimensions == 3
129 const int sourceSize = (sourcePatchSize + 2 * sourceHaloSize)
130 * (sourcePatchSize + 2 * sourceHaloSize)
131 * (sourcePatchSize + 2 * sourceHaloSize)
132 * NumberOfUnknowns;
133 const int destinationSize
134 = (destinationPatchSize + 2 * destinationHaloSize)
135 * (destinationPatchSize + 2 * destinationHaloSize)
136 * (destinationPatchSize + 2 * destinationHaloSize) * NumberOfUnknowns;
137#elif Dimensions == 2
138 const int sourceSize = (sourcePatchSize + 2 * sourceHaloSize)
139 * (sourcePatchSize + 2 * sourceHaloSize)
140 * NumberOfUnknowns;
141 const int destinationSize
142 = (destinationPatchSize + 2 * destinationHaloSize)
143 * (destinationPatchSize + 2 * destinationHaloSize) * NumberOfUnknowns;
144#endif
145
146 double sourceData[sourceSize];
147 for (int i = 0; i < sourceSize; i++)
148 sourceData[i] = i;
149
150 double destinationDataLinear[destinationSize];
151 double destinationDataSecondOrder[destinationSize];
152
153 interpolateCellDataAssociatedToVolumesIntoOverlappingCell_linear(
154 sourcePatchSize,
155 destinationPatchSize,
156 sourceHaloSize,
157 destinationHaloSize,
158 NumberOfUnknowns,
159 sourceData,
160 destinationDataLinear
161 );
162
163 interpolateCellDataAssociatedToVolumesIntoOverlappingCell_secondOrder(
164 sourcePatchSize,
165 destinationPatchSize,
166 sourceHaloSize,
167 destinationHaloSize,
168 NumberOfUnknowns,
169 sourceData,
170 destinationDataSecondOrder
171 );
172
173 int sourceWidth = sourcePatchSize + 2 * sourceHaloSize;
174 int destinationWidth = destinationPatchSize + 2 * destinationHaloSize;
175 double patchRatio = (double)sourcePatchSize / destinationPatchSize;
176
177#if Dimensions == 3
178 double offset1 = ((double)sourceHaloSize - 0.5 - 0.5 * patchRatio)
179 * sourceWidth * sourceWidth
180 + ((double)sourceHaloSize - 0.5 - 0.5 * patchRatio
181 ) * sourceWidth
182 + ((double)sourceHaloSize - 0.5 - 0.5 * patchRatio);
183#elif Dimensions == 2
184 double offset1 = ((double)sourceHaloSize - 0.5 - 0.5 * patchRatio
185 ) * sourceWidth
186 + ((double)sourceHaloSize - 0.5 - 0.5 * patchRatio);
187#endif
188
189#if Dimensions == 3
190 double offset2 = 0.0;
191 for (int k = 0; k < destinationWidth; k++) {
192#endif
193 double offset3 = 0.0;
194 for (int j = 0; j < destinationWidth; j++) {
195 for (int i = 0; i < destinationWidth; i++) {
196 int outsidePatchAlongCoordinateAxis = 0;
197 if (i < destinationHaloSize)
198 outsidePatchAlongCoordinateAxis++;
199 if (i >= destinationPatchSize + destinationHaloSize)
200 outsidePatchAlongCoordinateAxis++;
201 if (j < destinationHaloSize)
202 outsidePatchAlongCoordinateAxis++;
203 if (j >= destinationPatchSize + destinationHaloSize)
204 outsidePatchAlongCoordinateAxis++;
205#if Dimensions == 3
206 if (k < destinationHaloSize)
207 outsidePatchAlongCoordinateAxis++;
208 if (k >= destinationPatchSize + destinationHaloSize)
209 outsidePatchAlongCoordinateAxis++;
210#endif
211 if (outsidePatchAlongCoordinateAxis <= 1) {
212#if Dimensions == 3
213 int index = i + j * destinationWidth
214 + k * destinationWidth * destinationWidth;
215 validateNumericalEqualsWithEpsWithParams1(
216 destinationDataSecondOrder[index],
217 offset1 + offset2 + offset3 + patchRatio * i,
218 0.0001,
219 index
220 );
221#elif Dimensions == 2
222 int index = i + j * destinationWidth;
223 validateNumericalEqualsWithEpsWithParams1(
224 destinationDataSecondOrder[index],
225 offset1 + offset3 + patchRatio * i,
226 0.0001,
227 index
228 );
229#endif
230 }
231 }
232 offset3 += (double)sourceWidth * patchRatio;
233 }
234
235#if Dimensions == 3
236 offset2 += (double)sourceWidth * sourceWidth * patchRatio;
237 }
238#endif
239 }
240 }
